<p>A <b>stick</b> is an item used for <a href="/w/Crafting" title="Crafting">crafting</a> many <a class="mw-redirect" href="/w/Tools" title="Tools">tools</a> and <a href="/w/Item" title="Item">items</a>.
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Fishing">Fishing</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="/w/Stick?section=3&amp;veaction=edit" title="Edit section: Fishing">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/Stick?action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Fishing">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Sticks can be obtained as a "junk" item while <a href="/w/Fishing" title="Fishing">fishing</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Block_loot">Block loot</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="/w/Stick?section=4&amp;veaction=edit" title="Edit section: Block loot">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/Stick?action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Block loot">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><a class="mw-redirect" href="/w/Dead_bush" title="Dead bush">Dead bushes</a> drop between 0–2 sticks when destroyed.
</p><p>All <a href="/w/Leaves" title="Leaves">leaf</a> types have a 2% chance to drop between 1-2 sticks when broken. Using a tool with <a href="/w/Fortune" title="Fortune">Fortune</a> increase these chances to 2.2%, 2.5%, and 3.3% for Fortune I, II, and III respectively.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Entity_loot">Entity loot</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="/w/Stick?section=5&amp;veaction=edit" title="Edit section: Entity loot">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/Stick?action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Entity loot">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><a href="/w/Witch" title="Witch">Witches</a> have a chance of dropping 0–6 sticks upon death. This is increased by 3 per level of <a href="/w/Looting" title="Looting">Looting</a>, for a chance of 0-15 sticks.
</p><p><a href="/w/Boat" title="Boat">Boats</a> and <a href="/w/Boat_with_Chest" title="Boat with Chest">boats with chests</a> drop 2 sticks when falling from exactly 12, 13, 49, 51, 111, 114, 198, 202, 310, or 315 blocks.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup>.
</p>

</td>
<td>In <a href="/w/Bedrock_Edition" title="Bedrock Edition"><i>Bedrock Edition</i></a>, grindstone recipes built with crimson, warped, or mangrove planks can use a slab of almost any of the stone types including sandstone, quartz, and bricks.<sup class="noprint nowrap Inline-Template" title="">[<i><a class="text" href="https://minecraft.wiki/w/Talk:Stick"><span style="border-bottom: 1px dotted" title="Which slabs specifically?">more information needed</span></a></i>]</sup>
</td></tr>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Fuel">Fuel</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="/w/Stick?section=9&amp;veaction=edit" title="Edit section: Fuel">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/Stick?action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Fuel">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>When used as a <a href="/w/Furnace" title="Furnace">furnace</a> fuel, a stick smelts 0.5 <a href="/w/Item" title="Item">items</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Trading">Trading</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="/w/Stick?section=10&amp;veaction=edit" title="Edit section: Trading">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/Stick?action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Trading">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Novice-level <a href="/w/Trading#Fletcher" title="Trading">fletcher</a> <a href="/w/Villager" title="Villager">villagers</a> have a <sup>2</sup>⁄<sub>3</sub> chance to buy 32 sticks for an <a href="/w/Emerald" title="Emerald">emerald</a> in <i>Java Edition</i>, and they always offer the trade in Bedrock Edition.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Issues">Issues</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="/w/Stick?section=15&amp;veaction=edit" title="Edit section: Issues">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/Stick?action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Issues">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Issues relating to "Stick" are maintained on the <a href="/w/Bug_tracker" title="Bug tracker">bug tracker</a>. Report issues <a class="external text" href="https://bugs.mojang.com/issues/?jql=project%20in%20%28MC%2C%20MCPE%29%20and%20%28resolution%20is%20empty%20or%20resolution%20in%20%281%2C%202%2C%206%29%29%20and%20%28summary%20~%20%22Stick%22%29%20order%20by%20resolution%20desc" rel="nofollow noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">there</a>.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Trivia">Trivia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="/w/Stick?section=16&amp;veaction=edit" title="Edit section: Trivia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/Stick?action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Trivia">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>The stick is used in 49 recipes in <i>Java Edition</i>, and 50 recipes in <i>Bedrock Edition</i>, more than any other item in the game. <a class="mw-redirect" href="/w/Iron_ingot" title="Iron ingot">Iron ingot</a> takes second place with 35 recipes, and <a href="/w/Planks" title="Planks">planks</a> take third place with 34 recipes.</li>
<li>To craft each recipe once, a player would need 111 sticks, including 1 for the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/w/Redstone_torch" title="Redstone torch">redstone torch</a> in an <a class="mw-redirect" href="/w/Activator_rail" title="Activator rail">activator rail</a>, while using the extra tripwire hook for the <a href="/w/Crossbow" title="Crossbow">crossbow</a>. This would require 56 <a href="/w/Planks" title="Planks">planks</a>, or 14 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/w/Logs" title="Logs">logs</a>, for the sticks, and an extra 29 planks for the <a href="/w/Tool" title="Tool">wooden tools</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/w/Tripwire_hook" title="Tripwire hook">tripwire hook</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/w/Signs" title="Signs">signs</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/w/Fences" title="Fences">fences</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/w/Fence_gate" title="Fence gate">fence gate</a>, <a href="/w/Grindstone" title="Grindstone">grindstone</a>, and slabs for the <a href="/w/Barrel" title="Barrel">barrel</a>. This means that the player needs a total of 85 planks, or 22 logs, plus 6 more for the <a href="/w/Campfire" title="Campfire">campfire</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/w/Soul_campfire" title="Soul campfire">soul campfire</a>.</li></ul>
